country_event = { # GER: AUS is back!
	id = gerflavor.0
	title = gerflavor.0.t
	desc = gerflavor.0.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_anschluss
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerflavor.0"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # yay!
		name = gerflavor.0.a
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavor.0 option gerflavor.0.a"
		set_temp_variable = { ruling_party_pop_to_increase = 0.1 }
		increase_ruling_party_pop_by_num = yes
		add_war_support = 0.1
		AUS = { 
			4 = { add_claim_by = GER }
			39 = { add_claim_by = GER }
			152 = { add_claim_by = GER }
			153 = { add_claim_by = GER }
			803 = { add_claim_by = GER }
			912 = { add_claim_by = GER }
			913 = { add_claim_by = GER }
			enable_country_integration_50_compliance = yes 
		}
		if = {
			limit = { GER_is_cultural_revolution_started = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { amount = 5 }
			GER_add_social_outlook = yes
			set_temp_variable = { amount = 10 }
			GER_add_reichs_morale = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GER_helped_AUS_tst }
			clr_country_flag = GER_helped_AUS_tst
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_in_array = { GER.region_states@osterreich = THIS } }
				add_compliance = 5
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = GER_tst_terror
					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GER_helped_AUS_yc }
			clr_country_flag = GER_helped_AUS_yc
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_in_array = { GER.region_states@osterreich = THIS } }
				add_compliance = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # rochling
	id = gerflavor.1
	title = gerflavor.1.t
	desc = gerflavor.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_rochling
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerflavor.1"}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		controls_state = 981
		RHI = { 
			OR = {
				exists = no
				has_capitulated = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 45
	}

	option = { # yay?
		name = gerflavor.1.a
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavor.1 option gerflavor.1.a"
		981 = { 
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_used_rochling
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_industrial_concern
		show_ideas_tooltip = rochling 
	}
	
	option = { # yay?
		name = gerflavor.1.b
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavor.1 option gerflavor.1.b"
		add_political_power = 25
		if = {
			limit = { GER_is_cultural_revolution_started = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { amount = 5 }
			GER_add_social_outlook = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # GER: Valkists in AUS
	id = gerflavor.2
	title = gerflavor.2.t
	desc = gerflavor.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_reschny
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerflavor.2"}

	option = { # yay?
		name = gerflavor.2.a
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavor.2 option gerflavor.2.a"
		add_manpower = -2500
		custom_effect_tooltip = gerflavor.2.tt
		set_country_flag = GER_helped_AUS_valkists
	}
	
	option = { # yay?
		name = gerflavor.2.b
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavor.2 option gerflavor.2.b"
		add_political_power = 75
		if = {
			limit = { GER_is_cultural_revolution_started = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { amount = -2.5 }
			GER_add_reichs_morale = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # expansion of wehrmacht academy
	id = germil.2
	title = germil.2.t
	desc = germil.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_blomberg_fritsch
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germil.2"}
	trigger = { has_idea = GER_wehrmacht_academy }

	option = { # nice
		name = germil.2.a
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germil.2 option germil.2.a"
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_wehrmacht_academy
			add_idea = GER_wehrmacht_academy_better
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # securing that military
	id = germil.6
	title = germil.6.t
	desc = germil.6.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_reichswehr_nice
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germil.6"}

	option = { # ahhhhhhhh
		name = germil.6.a
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germil.6 option germil.6.a"
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_bribes_threats_promises
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GER_Gerd_von_Rundstedt }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = GER_convert_rundstedt }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GER_Gunther_von_Kluge }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = GER_convert_kluge }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GER_Fedor_von_Bock }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = GER_convert_bock }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GER_Ritter_von_Leeb }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = GER_convert_leeb }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GER_Ewald_von_Kleist }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = GER_convert_kleist }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GER_Ludwig_Beck }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = GER_convert_beck }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GER_Werner_von_Fritsch }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = GER_convert_fritsch }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GER_Walther_von_Brauchitsch }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = GER_convert_brauchitsch }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GER_Franz_Halder }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = GER_convert_halder }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # reichenau as chief
	id = germil.7
	title = germil.7.t
	desc = germil.7.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_Reichenau
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germil.7"}

	option = { # mmmmmmm no
		name = germil.7.a
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germil.7 option germil.7.a"
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = valkist 
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
		ROOT = {
			GER_Walther_von_Reichenau = {
				set_character_flag = {
					flag = GER_just_got_firednau
					days = 180
					value = 1
				}
			}
			deactivate_advisor = GER_Walther_von_Reichenau_carm
		}
	}
	
	option = { # fuck em'
		name = germil.7.b
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germil.7 option germil.7.b"
		add_command_power = -100
		add_political_power = -50
		random_list = {
			4 = { } # nothing...
			5 = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					retire_character = GER_Gerd_von_Rundstedt
					retire_character = GER_Erwin_von_Witzleben
					retire_character = GER_Ritter_von_Leeb
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					GER_Gerd_von_Rundstedt = { set_nationality = XXB set_character_flag = GER_retired_general }
					GER_Erwin_von_Witzleben = { set_nationality = XXB set_character_flag = GER_retired_general }
					GER_Ritter_von_Leeb = { set_nationality = XXB set_character_flag = GER_retired_general }
				}			
			}
		}
	}
}

	}
}

unit_leader_event = { # loyalty...
	id = germil.12
	title = germil.12.t
	desc = germil.12.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germil.12"
		hidden_effect = { GER_determine_general_preference = yes }
	}

	option = { # but prussia!!!!!!!
		name = germil.12.a
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germil.12 option germil.12.a"
		add_command_power = 25
		ROOT = { 
			random_list = {
				5 = { } # nothing...
				5 = {
					modifier = { 
						multiply_temp_variable = { GER_very_prussian = 2 }
						add = GER_very_prussian
					}
					modifier = { 
						multiply_temp_variable = { GER_traditional_outlook = 1.5 }
						add = GER_traditional_outlook
					}
					modifier = {
						multiply_temp_variable = { GER_revolutionary_outlook = -1.2 }
						add = GER_revolutionary_outlook
					}
					modifier = {
						has_completed_focus = GER_yc_valkist_compromise_army
						add = 4
					}
					modifier = {
						has_completed_focus = GER_legacy_of_schleichers_betrayal
						add = 10
					}
					modifier = {
						has_country_flag = GER_yc_cooperated_with_reichswehr_cliques
						add = -2
					}
					remove_unit_leader_trait = hidden_sympathies
					PREV = { GER_military_loyalty_cr_check = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # bribes
		name = germil.12.b
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germil.12 option germil.12.b"
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GER_likes_money > 3 } }
			add_political_power = -125
		}
		else = { add_political_power = -100 }
		ROOT = { 
			random_list = {
				5 = { } # nothing...
				6 = {
					modifier = { 
						multiply_temp_variable = { GER_likes_money = 2.5 }
						add = GER_likes_money
					}
					modifier = {
						has_completed_focus = GER_legacy_of_schleichers_betrayal
						add = 5
					}
					modifier = {
						has_country_flag = GER_yc_cooperated_with_reichswehr_cliques
						add = -2
					}
					remove_unit_leader_trait = hidden_sympathies
					PREV = { GER_military_loyalty_cr_check = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # promise church niceness
		name = germil.12.c
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_prohibited_catholics } }
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germil.12 option germil.12.c"
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.04
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = valkist 
			popularity = -0.06
		}

country_event = { # Companies Relocates to the Rhineland/Kiel
	id = gerdom.25
	title = gerdom.25.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_industry
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.25"}

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			country_exists = SHO
			country_exists = RHI
		}
		text = gerdom.25.d.main
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			country_exists = RHI
			NOT = { country_exists = SHO }
		}
		text = gerdom.25.d.rhine
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			country_exists = SHO
			NOT = { country_exists = RHI }
		}
		text = gerdom.25.d.kiel
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			country_exists = RHI
			country_exists = SHO
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerdom.25 option gerdom.25.a"
		name = gerdom.25.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = RHI }
				RHI = { country_event = gerdom.26 }
				set_global_flag = GER_companies_evacuated_rhine
			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = SHO }
				SHO = { country_event = gerdom.26 }
				set_global_flag = GER_companies_evacuated_kiel
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # good kk end
	id = gerdom.52
	title = gerdom.52.t
	desc = gerdom.52.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_kirchenkampf
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gerdom.52"}

	option = { # oh yeah
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerdom.52 option gerdom.52.a"
		name = gerdom.52.a
		add_stability = 0.1
		if = {
			limit = { GER_is_cultural_revolution_started = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { amount = 15 }
			GER_add_social_outlook = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = valkist }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_kirchenkampf_spirit
				add_idea = GER_zeitgeist_victory
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GER_chose_dinter }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_kirchenkampf_spirit
				add_idea = GER_spiritual_revival
			}
			clr_country_flag = GER_chose_dinter
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GER_chose_hauer }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_kirchenkampf_spirit
				add_idea = GER_german_faith
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_kirchenkampf_spirit
				add_idea = GER_german_christianity
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = gertst.7
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gertst.7" }
	title = gertst.7.t
	desc = gertst.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_rosenberg
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = gertst.7.a # let meyer in
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gertst.7 option gertst.7.a"
		add_political_power = 50
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = national_populist 
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_country_with_original_tag = {
						original_tag_to_check = UKR 
						is_in_array = { global.GER_reichslander = THIS }
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = GER_meyer_rosenberg
		}
		else = {
			every_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = UKR 
				limit = { is_in_array = { global.GER_reichslander = THIS } }
				GER = {
					GER_Alfred_Meyer = {
						set_nationality = PREV
					}
					
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gertst.8 days = 365 random_days = 120 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = gertst.7.b # he is "indispensable"
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gertst.7 option gertst.7.b"
		add_war_support = -0.02
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = national_populist 
			popularity = -0.06
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gertst.8 days = 365 random_days = 120 } }
		set_country_flag = GER_rosenberg_weaker
	}
}

country_event = { # bamberg conference
	id = gertst.14
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event gertst.14" }
	title = gertst.14.t
	desc = gertst.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_tst_conference
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = gertst.14.a # jung gets kill
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					set_temp_variable = { valk_ratio = party_popularity_100@valkist }
					divide_temp_variable = { valk_ratio = party_popularity_100@national_populist }
					check_variable = { valk_ratio > 0.64 }
				}
				GER = { has_country_leader = { character = GER_Hermann_Gauch } }
			}
		}
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gertst.14 option gertst.14.a"
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = valkist
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = { 
				GER_Rudolf_Jung = { retire = yes }
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = GER_Rudolf_Jung
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = GER_Hermann_Gauch } } }
			promote_character = GER_Hermann_Gauch
			activate_advisor = GER_Friedrich_Schmitt_sec_npo
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = GER_Viktor_Lutze
					activate = yes
					advisor = {
						slot = head_of_government
						cost = 100
						idea_token = GER_Viktor_Lutze_hog_npo
						traits = {
							national_populist
							hog_happy_amateur
						}
					}
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = { activate_advisor = GER_Viktor_Lutze_hog_npo }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GER_lutze_shall_get_purged }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gertst.24 days = 20 } }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = gertst.22 days = 20 } } }
		set_temp_variable = { amount = 10 }
		GER_add_social_outlook = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = gertst.14.b # gauch shall go!
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					set_temp_variable = { natpop_ratio = party_popularity_100@national_populist }
					divide_temp_variable = { natpop_ratio = party_popularity_100@valkist }
					check_variable = { natpop_ratio > 0.64 }
				}
				GER = { has_country_leader = { character = GER_Rudolf_Jung } }
			}
		}
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gertst.14 option gertst.14.b"
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = national_populist 
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = valkist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:valkist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = { 
				GER_Hermann_Gauch = { retire = yes }
				GER_Wolf_von_Helldorff = { set_nationality = ROOT }
				activate_advisor = GER_Wolf_von_Helldorff_sec_npo
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = GER_Hermann_Gauch
			activate_advisor = GER_Wolf_von_Helldorff_sec_npo
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = GER_Rudolf_Jung } } }
			promote_character = GER_Rudolf_Jung
			hidden_effect = {
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = GER_Viktor_Lutze
					activate = yes
					advisor = {
						slot = head_of_government
						cost = 100
						idea_token = GER_Viktor_Lutze_hog_npo
						traits = {
							national_populist
							hog_happy_amateur
						}
					}
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = { activate_advisor = GER_Viktor_Lutze_hog_npo }
		}
		set_country_leader_ideology = volkisch_national_valkism_subtype
		add_stability = -0.05
		set_temp_variable = { amount = 10 }
		GER_add_reichs_morale = yes
	}
}

# HIDDEN
# the following events are hidden and mainly used for code purposes

#TODO FIGURE OUT A WAY TO DO IT WITH ONE EVENT AND NO FLAGS!! FLAGS ARE CRINGE
country_event = { # #Propaganda Dispatcher - Used to update Campaign GFX to old-er strips
	id = gerhidden.1
	title = gerhidden.1.t
	desc = gerhidden.1.d
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		#So that this does not happen if a propaganda is cancelled, breaking everything
		any_of = {
			array = GER_propaganda_slots_to_age
			value = v
			meta_trigger = {
				text = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = { flag = GER_propaganda_age_[v] days = 45 } } }
				debug = yes
				v = "[?v]"
			}
			check_variable = { age@var:v > 2 }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		for_each_loop = {
			array = GER_propaganda_slots_to_age
			value = v
			log = "IMMEDIATE FOR LOOP: V: [?v]"
			if = { 
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { var = age@var:v value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } } } 
				meta_effect = {
					text = { set_country_flag = { flag = GER_propaganda_age_[v] days = 45 } log = "FLAG: [?GER_propaganda_age_1:days_left|Y0]" }
					debug = yes
					v = "[?v]"
				}
				country_event = { id = gerhidden.1 days = 45 }
				add_to_variable = { GER_propaganda_dirty = 1 }
			} else = {
				# do nothing, the decision should remove it...
				add_to_variable = { GER_propaganda_dirty = 1 }
				remove_from_array = { GER_propaganda_slots_to_age = var:v }
			}
		}
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gerhidden.6
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					check_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_pp_gain > 0.15 }
					GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_modern_authoritarian_state }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_pp_gain = 0.01 } # base gain of 0.1 PP gain
			if = {
				limit = { valkist > 0.55 }
				add_to_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_pp_gain = 0.01 } # additional gain of 0.1 PP gain
			}
			if = {
				limit = { valkist > 0.65 }
				add_to_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_pp_gain = 0.01 } # additional gain of 0.1 PP gain
			}
			if = {
				limit = { valkist > 0.8 }
				add_to_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_pp_gain = 0.02 } # additional gain of 0.2 PP gain
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					check_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_stability_factor > 0.15 }
					GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_modern_authoritarian_state }
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_stability_factor = 0.002 } # base gain of 0.2% stability
			if = {
				limit = { valkist > 0.55 }
				add_to_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_stability_factor = 0.001 } # additional gain of 0.1% stability
			}
			if = {
				limit = { valkist > 0.65 }
				add_to_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_stability_factor = 0.001 } # additional gain of 0.1% stability
			}
			if = {
				limit = { valkist > 0.8 }
				add_to_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_stability_factor = 0.001 } # additional gain of 0.1% stability
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_pp_gain > 0.15 }
						check_variable = { GER_legalized_dictatorship_stability_factor > 0.15 }
					}
					GER = { has_completed_focus = GER_modern_authoritarian_state }
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = gerhidden.6 days = 30 } # monthly!
		}
	}
}

	}

					ITA = { has_capitulated = no }
				}
			}
		}
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerexp.27 option gerexp.27.a"
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.balkans_tags_array
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_ally_with = GER } }
				GER = { PREV = { country_event = { id = gerexp.3 days = 2 } } }

		}

			ENG = { has_war = no }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = gerexp.49.d
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = gerexp.49.a # cool

			NOT = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = GER
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerexp.49 option gerexp.49.a"
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ENG }
			leave_faction = yes
			create_faction = imperial_protection_alliance
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GEN_GER_former_faction_member }
				ENG = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
			clr_country_flag = GEN_GER_former_faction_leader
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = gerexp.49.b # sad!

			original_tag = GER
			has_war = yes
		}
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerexp.49 option gerexp.49.b"
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = hostile_status }
	}
}

	trigger = {
		AND = {
			original_tag = ENG

		}

				}

							controls_state = PREV
						}
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}

				limit = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_on_continent = europe
					is_controlled_by = ENG

							}

									size > 0

								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				GER = {

				}
				else = {

	}
